<script type="text/javascript">
$.views.converters("humanperiod", function($val) {
    if ($val.match(/1Y/)) { return $val.replace(/Y/g, ' Year'); }
    if ($val.match(/Y/)) { return $val.replace(/Y/g, ' Years'); }
    if ($val.match(/1M/)) { return $val.replace(/M/g, ' Month'); }
    if ($val.match(/M/)) { return $val.replace(/M/g, ' Months'); }
    return $val;
});
</script>

<script id="domain_period" type="text/x-jsrender">
<option value="{{:period}}">{{humanperiod:period}} @ {{if price == "0.00"}}FREE{{else}}{{:currency}} {{:price}}{{/if}} </option>
</script>

			        jQuery(function($) {
			            var domainConfigurationForm = $('[data-domain-configuration-form]');
			            var idshieldChecker = $('[data-domain-configuration-idshield]');
			            var domainConfigurationSubmit = $("#configure_submit_button");

			            idshieldChecker.change(function() {
			                domainConfigurationForm.find('.alert').remove();

			                if (!idshieldChecker.is(':checked')) {
			                    //domainConfigurationSubmit.after('<div class="alert alert-error">You can only proceed by accepting our IDShield Terms and Conditions (stated below)</div>');
			                }
			            });

			            domainConfigurationForm.submit(function(e) {
                            if ($(".idshield-container:visible").size() > 0) {
                                domainConfigurationForm.find('.alert').remove();
                                if (!idshieldChecker.is(':checked')) {
                                    e.preventDefault();
                                    domainConfigurationSubmit.after('<div class="alert alert-error">You can only proceed by accepting our IDShield Terms and Conditions (stated above)</div>');
                                }
                            }
			            });
			        });
			    </script>

			    <h1>Freenom ID Shield WHOIS Privacy Service Agreement</h1>

			    <ol>

			            <ol>
			                <li>This Freenom ID Shield WHOIS Privacy Service Agreement ("Privacy Service Agreement") sets forth the terms and conditions of your use of the services offered by Stichting OpenTLD WHOIS Proxy, a Dutch foundation, ("ID Shield") and OpenTLD B.V., A Dutch corporation ("Freenom") pursuant to the Services Agreement by and between ID Shield and Freenom, wherein ID Shield agrees to provide consumers of Freenom's domain name registration and hosting services ("Freenom Registrant") with WHOIS privacy protection services ("ID Shield Services Agreement").</li>
			                <li>This Privacy Service Agreement serves to supplement your Domain Registration Agreement and/or Hosting Services Agreement between you on the one hand and Freenom on the other hand, and which is incorporated herein by reference. In this Privacy Service Agreement "you" and "your" refer to you or any agent, employee, servant or person authorized to act on your behalf, and the Freenom Registrant listed in the WHOIS contact information for the domain name. This Privacy Service Agreement explains Freenom's obligations to you in connection with your WHOIS privacy protection services, and explains your obligations to Freenom for privacy protection services offered by third party ID Shield under the ID Shield Services Agreement.</li>
			            </ol>
			        </li>
			        <li>FREENOM ID SHIELD PRIVACY SERVICES
			            <ol>
			                <li>By subscribing to the Freenom WHOIS Privacy Protection Services ("WHOIS Privacy Services"), you are engaging ID Shield to administer and register each domain name controlled by you ("Protected Domain") in the name of ID Shield. Thus, your name, postal address, email address, phone and fax numbers shall be kept confidential, subject to this Privacy Service Agreement. The following information (and not your personal information) will be made publicly available in the WHOIS directory for each Protected Domain:
			                    <ol>
			                        <li>An account specific ID Shield email address, and ID Shield postal address and phone and facsimile number for the registrant, administrative, technical, and billing contacts ("ID Shield Addresses");</li>
			                        <li>The primary and secondary domain name servers you designate for the Protected Domain;</li>
			                        <li>The Protected Domain's original date of registration and expiration date; and</li>
			                        <li>The identity of your registrar, domain name service provider (if different from registrar) and the status of the Protected Domain with the registrar (such as, "active," "Registrar Lock," "clienthold," etc.).</li>
			                    </ol>
			                </li>
			            </ol>
			        </li>
			        <li>YOUR RIGHTS
			            <ol>

			                <li>You will retain the right to sell, transfer, or assign each Protected Domain.</li>
			                <li>You will retain the right to control and set the DNS settings for the Protected Domain(s).</li>
			                <li>You will retain the right to renew each Protected Domain name registration upon expiration (subject to Freenom's applicable rules and policies).</li>
			                <li>You will remain responsible to resolve any and all monetary or other legal claims that arise in connection with your Protected Domain(s), subject to the remaining provisions of this Privacy Service Agreement, the ID Shield Services Agreement, and your Domain Registration Agreement and/or Hosting Services Agreement with Freenom (collectively, "Agreements").

			            </ol>
			        </li>
			    </ol>
			    <li>YOUR PERSONAL INFORMATION
			        <ol>
			            <li>You agree that for each Protected Domain, you will provide to ID Shield and maintain as current and accurate, the following information:
			                <ol>
			                    <li>Your name, address, email address, postal address, phone and fax numbers;</li>
			                    <li>The name, address, email address, postal address, phone and fax numbers for the Protected Domain's administrative, technical, and billing contacts; and</li>
			                    <li>The primary and secondary domain name servers for the Protected Domain.</li>
			                </ol>
			            </li>
			            <li>You agree to:
			                <ol>
			                    <li>Update this information immediately as it changes over time;</li>
			                    <li>Respond within five (5) business days to any inquiries made by ID Shield to determine the validity of personal information provided by you;</li>
			                    <li>Promptly respond to messages regarding correspondence addressed to or involving your Protected Domain(s), as more fully set forth below.</li>
			                </ol>
			            </li>
			            <li>If you do not supply primary and secondary domain name servers, you agree that ID Shield or Freenom may point your Protected Domain(s) to an IP address of its choosing until such time as you supply primary and secondary domain name servers.</li>
			        </ol>
			    </li>
			    <li>RENEWAL AND FEES
			        <ol>
			            <li>If you have selected automatic renewal of the WHOIS Privacy Services administered by ID Shield, you agree:
			                <ol>
			                    <li>That the WHOIS Privacy Services shall be automatically renewed 30 days prior to the end of term of your Domain Name Registration Agreement or Hosting Services Agreement with Freenom;</li>
			                    <li>That ID Shield will attempt to charge your Freenom account at the then current rates;</li>
			                    <li>That you waive any requirement to obtain your ongoing affirmative consent to any such automatic renewal.</li>
			                </ol>

jQuery(document).ready(function(){


    $('#tgr').poshytip({
        className: 'idshield-tooltip-container',
        showOn: 'none',
        alignTo: 'target',
        alignX: 'center',
        alignY: 'bottom',
        offsetX: 0,
        offsetY: 5,
        showTimeout: 100
    });
    var tooltipIsShown = false;
    $('#tgr').click(function() {
        if(!tooltipIsShown){
            $('#tgr').poshytip('show');
            tooltipIsShown = true
        } else {
            $('#tgr').poshytip('hide');
            tooltipIsShown = false;
        }
        return false;
    }).mouseleave(function(){
        $('#tgr').poshytip('hideDelayed', 400);
        tooltipIsShown = false;
    });

    $('#tos-full').hide();
    var tosOpen = false;
    $('.tos').removeClass('active');

    $('.tos-trigger').on('click', function(){
        if (tosOpen){
            $('.tos').removeClass('active');
            $('#tos-full').slideUp();
            
            tosOpen = false;
        } else {
            $('.tos').addClass('active');
            $('#tos-full').slideDown();
            
            tosOpen = true;
        }
        return false;
    });
});

$(function() {

    // load periods and prices {{{
    function load_periods_and_prices() {
        var $domains = [];
        $(".tableDomain").each(function() {
            $domains.push($.trim($(this).text()));
        });

        // post delete of domain
        $.ajax({
            url:    "/includes/domains/confdomain-pricing.php",
            type:   'post',
            data:   { domains: $domains },
            crossDomain: true,
            beforeSend: function(xhr) { xhr.withCredentials = true; },
            xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
            success: function($data, $status) {

                // foreach domain
                for (var $domain in $data) {
                    if ($data.hasOwnProperty($domain)) {

                        // lowercase domain & replace . with _
                        $domain_str = $domain.toLowerCase();
                        $domain_str = $domain_str.replace('.', '_');

                        // add select + options via rendering.

                        // build the HTML pull down code
                        var $tmpl = $.templates("#domain_period");
                        var $options = $tmpl.render($data[$domain].pricing);

                        var $initial_period = $("#" + $domain_str + "_period_text").attr("initial") + 'Y';
                        $initial_period = $initial_period.replace('MY', 'M');
                        $initial_period = $initial_period.replace('U', '');

                        $("#" + $domain_str + "_period_text").html(
                            "<select class='select_period' name='" + $domain_str + "_period'>" + $options + "</select>"
                        );
                        $("[name='" + $domain_str + "_period']").val($initial_period);
                    }
                }

                // update domain period in cart
                $(".select_period").change(function() {
                    var $domain_str = $(this).attr('name');
                    var $period = $(this).val();
                    var $domain = $domain_str.replace('_period', '');
                    $domain     = $domain.replace('_', '.');
                    $domain     = $domain.toLowerCase();

                    if ($period.match(/M/g)) {
                        $(this).parent().parent().parent().find(".idShield").hide('slow', function(){ show_idshield(); });
                    } else {
                        $(this).parent().parent().parent().find(".idShield").show('slow', function(){ show_idshield(); });
                    }

                    $.ajax({
                        url:    "/includes/domains/confdomain-update.php",
                        type:   'post',
                        data:   { domain: $domain, period: $period },
                        crossDomain: true,
                        beforeSend: function(xhr) { xhr.withCredentials = true; },
                        xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
                        success: function($data, $status) {
                        }
                    });
                });
                show_idshield();
            }
        });
    }
    // }}}

    // toggleSled {{{
    $('.idTogglerSled').click(function() {
        var $idshield = "enabled";
        var $domain = $(this).parent().parent().parent().find(".tableDomain").text();
        var $toggler = $(this);

        // we update only later, so now wrong = right.
        if ($(this).hasClass("active")) { $idshield = "disabled"; }

        $.ajax({
            url:    "/includes/domains/confdomain-update.php",
            type:   'post',
            data:   { domain: $domain, idshield: $idshield },
            crossDomain: true,
            beforeSend: function(xhr) { xhr.withCredentials = true; },
            xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
            success: function($data, $status) {
                $($toggler).toggleClass('active', function() {

                    // replace version of idshield
                    var $domain_str = $.trim($domain.toLowerCase());
                    $domain_str = $domain_str.replace('.', '_') + "_idprot";
                    if ($idshield == "enabled") {
                        $("#" + $domain_str).val("on");
                    } else {
                        $("#" + $domain_str).val("off");
                    }
                    show_idshield();
                });
            }
        });
    });
    // }}}
 
    // show_idshield() {{{   
    function show_idshield() {
        // determine nf or idshields on
        var $idshield = false;
        $(".idTogglerSled:visible").each(function() {
            if ($(this).hasClass("active")) {
                $idshield = true;
            }
        });

        if ($idshield) {
            $(".idshield-container").show();
        } else {
            $(".idshield-container").hide();
        }
    };
    // }}}

    // delete domains {{{
    $(".fa-minus-circle").click(function() {
        var $minus_pressed = $(this);
        var $domainname = $.trim($(this).parent().text());

        var $tmp = $domainname.split(".", 2);
        var $domain = $tmp[0];
        var $tld = "."+$tmp[1];

        // post delete of domain
        $.ajax({
            url:    "/includes/domains/fn-remove.php",
            type:   'post',
            data:   { domain: $domain, tld: $tld },
            crossDomain: true,
            beforeSend: function(xhr) { xhr.withCredentials = true; },
            xhrFields: { withCredentials: true },
            success: function($data, $status) {
                $minus_pressed.parent().parent().parent().remove();
                // how many domains are now left?
                if ($(".tableDomain").size() < 1) {
                    // hide the tables
                    $(".invoiceContent").hide();
            
                    var $link = $("#no_domains_page").val();
                    window.location.replace($link);
                }
                show_idshield();
            }
        });
    });
    // }}}
    
    // configure submit button {{{
    $("#configure_submit_button").click(function(e) {
        $domains = new Object;
        $(".errorMsg").hide();
        e.preventDefault();

        $(".hostname_input,.hostip_input,.dnsname_input,.dnsip_input,.forward_input").filter(':visible').each(function() {
            $parts  = $(this).attr("id").split("_");
            $domain = $parts[0];
            $attr   = $parts[1];

            if ( typeof($domains[$domain]) != 'object' ) {
                $domains[$domain] = new Object;
            }
            $domains[$domain][$attr] = $(this).val(); 
        });

        // post the info to domainconfigure.php
        $data_str = JSON.stringify($domains);
        $.post("/includes/domains/domainconfigure.php", { 
                data: $data_str
            }, function($data, $status) {
                // do something
                $res = JSON.parse($data);
                if ($res["status"] != "OK") {
                    $.each($res["errors"], function($k, $v) {
                        $k =  $k.replace('.', '_');
                        $('#error_' + $k).html($v);
                        $('#error_' + $k).show();
                    });
                } else {
                    $('[data-domain-configuration-form]').submit();
                }
            }
        );
    });
    // }}}

    // load prices
    load_periods_and_prices();
    show_idshield();
});

$(document).ready(function($){
	$('.useDNS').click(function(){ 
	    $(this).closest('li') // get current LI
	       .addClass('active')
	       .siblings() // get adjacent LIs
	       .removeClass('active');
	 
	       	
	       	if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>80 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<120 ) {
	       		$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:230},200);
	       	}
	       if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>10 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<50 ) {
       			$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:230},200);
       		}
       		if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>200 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<250 ) {
       				$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:32},200);
       			}

		});
	$('.useForward').click(function(){ 
	    $(this).closest('li') // get current LI
	       .addClass('active')
	       .siblings() // get adjacent LIs
	       .removeClass('active');
	   
	   	
		   if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>200 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<250 ) {
		   	$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:100},200);
		   }
	   		if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>10 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<50 ) {
	   			$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:100},200);
	   		}
	   		if($(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()>80 && $(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').height()<120 ) {
	   				$(this).closest('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:32},200);
	   		}
	});
	
	$('.useOwnDNS').click(function(){ 
	    $(this).closest('li') // get current LI
	       .addClass('active')
	       .siblings() // get adjacent LIs
	       .removeClass('active')
	});
	$('.useOurDNS').click(function(){ 
	    $(this).closest('li') // get current LI
	       .addClass('active')
	       .siblings() // get adjacent LIs
	       .removeClass('active')
	});
	
	$('.collapseAll').click(function(){ 
	   $('ul.useYourDomain').animate({height:32},200);
	});
		
});

<script type="text/javascript">
            

        function ioio() {
            var $v = ioGetBlackbox();
            // not entirely done? retry
            if (!$v.finished) {
                setTimeout(function(){ ioio(); }, 100);
            }
        }
        function fpio() {
            var $v = fpGetBlackbox();
            // not entirely done? retry
            if (!$v.finished) {
                setTimeout(function(){ fpio(); }, 100);
            }
        }
        $(function() {
            setTimeout(function(){ fpio(); }, 200);
            setTimeout(function(){ ioio(); }, 200);
        });

        
    </script>


<script type="text/javascript">

    $(function() {
        $('.submit-verifyemail').click(function() {
            grecaptcha.ready(function() {
                grecaptcha.execute(
                    '6LeRyJsUAAAAAOKmSY52HO3iBDz2QbXas2Q-kHjy',
                    {
                        action: 'cart_verifyemail'
                    }
                ).then(function(token) {

                    var input = $("<input>").attr("type", "hidden").attr("name", "captcha_tkn").val(token);
                    $('#verifyemailform').append(input).submit();
                });
            });
        });

        $('.submit-checkout').click(function() {
            if (!$("#accepttos").is(":checked")) {
                alert("Please read and agree to our terms and conditions");
            } else {
                grecaptcha.ready(function() {
                    grecaptcha.execute(
                        '6LeRyJsUAAAAAOKmSY52HO3iBDz2QbXas2Q-kHjy',
                        {
                            action: 'cart_submit_checkout_account'                        }
                    ).then(function(token) {

                        var input = $("<input>").attr("type", "hidden").attr("name", "captcha_tkn").val(token);
                        $('#mainfrm').append(input);

                        document.createElement('form').submit.call(mainfrm);
                    });
                });
            }
        });
    });
</script>

            $(this).removeClass('inputAlert');

    function removeItem(type,num) {
        var response = confirm("Are you sure you want to remove this item from your cart?");
        if (response) {
            window.location = 'cart.php?a=remove&r='+type+'&i='+num;
        }
    }
    function emptyCart(type,num) {
        var response = confirm("Are you sure you want to empty your shopping cart?");
        if (response) {
            window.location = 'cart.php?a=empty';
        }
    }
</script>

jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    jQuery("#existingcust").click(function(){
        if (jQuery(this).hasClass('active')!=true) {
			jQuery.fx.off = true;
            jQuery(".signuptype").removeClass('active');
            jQuery(this).addClass('active');
            jQuery("#signupfrm").fadeToggle('fast',function(){
                jQuery("#loginfrm").fadeToggle('fast');
            });
            jQuery("#custtype").val("existing");
        }
    });
    jQuery("#newcust").click(function(){
        if (jQuery(this).hasClass('active')!=true) {
		jQuery.fx.off = true;
            jQuery(".signuptype").removeClass('active');
            jQuery(this).addClass('active');
            jQuery("#loginfrm").fadeToggle('100',function(){
                jQuery("#signupfrm").fadeToggle('100');
            });
            jQuery("#custtype").val("new");
        }
    });

    jQuery("[data-processing-state]").closest('form').submit(function() {
        jQuery(this).find('[data-processing-state]').each(function() {
            var btn = jQuery(this);

            if (!btn.is(':disabled')) {
                btn.val(btn.data('processing-state'));
                btn.attr('disabled', true);
            }
        });
    });
});

function showcats() {
    jQuery("#categories").slideToggle();
}

function selproduct(num) {
    jQuery('#productslider').slider("value", num);
    jQuery(".product").hide();
    jQuery("#product"+num).show();
    jQuery(".sliderlabel").removeClass("selected");
    jQuery("#prodlabel"+num).addClass("selected");
}

function recalctotals() {
    jQuery.post("cart.php", 'ajax=1&a=confproduct&calctotal=true&'+jQuery("#orderfrm").serialize(),
    function(data){
        jQuery("#producttotal").html(data);
    });
}

function addtocart(gid) {
    jQuery("#loading1").slideDown();
    jQuery.post("cart.php", 'ajax=1&a=confproduct&'+jQuery("#orderfrm").serialize(),
    function(data){
        if (data) {
            jQuery("#configproducterror").html(data);
            jQuery("#configproducterror").slideDown();
            jQuery("#loading1").slideUp();
        } else {
            if (gid) window.location='cart.php?gid='+gid;
            else window.location='cart.php?a=confdomains';
        }
    });
}

function domaincontactchange() {
    if (jQuery("#domaincontact").val()=="addingnew") {
        jQuery("#domaincontactfields").slideDown();
    } else {
        jQuery("#domaincontactfields").slideUp();
    }
}

function showCCForm() {
    jQuery("#ccinputform").slideDown();
}
function hideCCForm() {
    jQuery("#ccinputform").slideUp();
}
function useExistingCC() {
    jQuery(".newccinfo").hide();
}
function enterNewCC() {
    jQuery(".newccinfo").show();
}

jQuery(document).ready(function(){

    jQuery("input[name=state]").attr("id","stateinput");

    jQuery("select[name=country]").change(function() {

        statechange();
        phoneccchange();
    });

    statechange();
        phoneccchange();

});

function statechange() {
    var state = jQuery("#stateinput").val();
    var country = jQuery("select[name=country]").val();
    if (typeof(statesTab) == "undefined") statesTab = '';
    if (states[country]) {
        jQuery("#stateinput").hide();
        jQuery("#stateinput").removeAttr("name");
        jQuery("#stateselect").remove();
        var stateops = '';
        $.each(states[country], function( key, value ) {
            stateops += '<option value="' + key + '"';
            if (key==state) stateops += ' selected="selected"'
            stateops += '>'+value+'</option>';
        });
        if(statesTab != '' && typeof(statesTab) != 'string') { statesTab = ' tabindex="'+statesTab+'"'; }
        jQuery("#stateinput").parent().append('<select name="state" id="stateselect"'+statesTab+'><option value="">Choose One...</option>'+stateops+'</select>');
    } else {
        jQuery("#stateselect").remove();
        jQuery("#stateinput").show();
        jQuery("#stateinput").attr("name","state");
    }
}

function phoneccchange() {
    var $country = jQuery("select[name=country]").val();
    if ($country == undefined) { return; }
    $(".countrycode").html('+' + $country_codes[$country]);
    var $l = 196 - ($country_codes[$country].length * 8);
    $(".input_box_phonenr").css("width", $l + 'px');
}

jQuery(document).ready(function(){
    if(typeof window.langPasswordWeak === 'undefined'){
        window.langPasswordWeak = "Weak";
    }
    if(typeof window.langPasswordModerate === 'undefined'){
        window.langPasswordModerate = "Moderate";
    }
    if(typeof window.langPasswordStrong === 'undefined'){
        window.langPasswordStrong = "Strong";
    }

    jQuery("#newpw").keyup(function () {
        var pwvalue = jQuery("#newpw").val();
        var pwstrength = getPasswordStrength(pwvalue);
        jQuery("#pwstrength").html(langPasswordStrong);
        jQuery("#pwstrengthpos").css("background-color","#33CC00");
        if (pwstrength<75) {
            jQuery("#pwstrength").html(langPasswordModerate);
            jQuery("#pwstrengthpos").css("background-color","#ff6600");
        }
        if (pwstrength<30) {
            jQuery("#pwstrength").html(langPasswordWeak);
            jQuery("#pwstrengthpos").css("background-color","#cc0000");
        }
        jQuery("#pwstrengthpos").css("width",1+pwstrength);
        jQuery("#pwstrengthneg").css("width",96-pwstrength);
    });
});

function getPasswordStrength(pw){
    var pwlength=(pw.length);
    if(pwlength>5)pwlength=5;
    var numnumeric=pw.replace(/[0-9]/g,"");
    var numeric=(pw.length-numnumeric.length);
    if(numeric>3)numeric=3;
    var symbols=pw.replace(/\W/g,"");
    var numsymbols=(pw.length-symbols.length);
    if(numsymbols>3)numsymbols=3;
    var numupper=pw.replace(/[A-Z]/g,"");
    var upper=(pw.length-numupper.length);
    if(upper>3)upper=3;
    var pwstrength=((pwlength*10)-20)+(numeric*10)+(numsymbols*15)+(upper*10);
    if(pwstrength<0){pwstrength=0}
    if(pwstrength>100){pwstrength=99}
    return pwstrength;
}

function showStrengthBar() {
    if(typeof window.langPasswordStrength === 'undefined'){
        window.langPasswordStrength = "Password Strength";
    }
    if(typeof window.langPasswordWeak === 'undefined'){
        window.langPasswordWeak = "Weak";
    }
    document.write('<table align="center" width="100%"><tr><td>'+langPasswordStrength+':</td><td width="105px"><div id="pwstrengthpos" style="position:relative;float:left;width:0px;background-color:#33CC00;border:1px solid #000;border-right:0px;">&nbsp;</div><div id="pwstrengthneg" style="position:relative;float:right;width:96px;background-color:#efefef;border:1px solid #000;border-left:0px;">&nbsp;</div></td><td><div id="pwstrength">'+langPasswordWeak+'</div></td></tr></table>');
}
